<div id="review_567723820" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/567723820" />
    <a title="Sunny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1022402-sunny"><img alt="Sunny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579287118p2/1022402.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/567723820?book_show_action=true">Mar 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sunny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sunny" href="/user/show/1022402-sunny">Sunny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1022402-sunny?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1022402-sunny?shelf=a-contemporary">a-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer567723820" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8430674087437797305">4.5 stars. This book rivals my favorite book by this author, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73086.Kiss_an_Angel' title='Kiss an Angel by Susan Elizabeth Phillips' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kiss an Angel</a>. I struggled through the first part of the book because I could not handle how mean the townsfolk were to our heroine. I didn't even like our hero too much because I really thought, given Rachel's dire circumstances, he was taking advantage of her. I had to put the book down for a few days, that's how upset I was. Once, I re-engaged and let the story progress, it was magic. <br/><br/>Rachel represents the kind of heroine I love fro</span>
  <span id="freeText8430674087437797305" style="display:none">4.5 stars. This book rivals my favorite book by this author, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/73086.Kiss_an_Angel" title="Kiss an Angel by Susan Elizabeth Phillips" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss an Angel</a>. I struggled through the first part of the book because I could not handle how mean the townsfolk were to our heroine. I didn't even like our hero too much because I really thought, given Rachel's dire circumstances, he was taking advantage of her. I had to put the book down for a few days, that's how upset I was. Once, I re-engaged and let the story progress, it was magic. <br /><br />Rachel represents the kind of heroine I love from this author. She is smart, a little naïve, stubborn as a mule, and with fortitude beyond measure. Yet, there is also an innocence that is utterly attractive. I wanted to hug her and tell her everything was going to be alright. Gabe is a slow burn for me. I certainly understand why he is so taciturn, but his manipulation bothers me. He keeps Rachel hanging for so long, it hurt. Ultimately, he is redeemed and I am satisfied, but it was not an easy ride. <br /><br />Again, like in her other books, the secondary characters are first rate. Gabe's brothers represent the very best and worst of a close-knit family. I adored Kristy and Ethan's story as much as Gabe and Rachel's. They say that you should never work with animals and kids because they steal the show. This holds true here. Edward is a scene stealer. Watching him bloom from an excruciatingly shy little boy to a rambunctious, inquisitive one is heart-warming. <br /><br />This one is another winner. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8430674087437797305" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_70419543" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/70419543" />
    <a title="Elle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2485186-elle"><img alt="Elle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352213985p2/2485186.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/70419543?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elle" href="/user/show/2485186-elle">Elle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485186-elle?shelf=sports-romance">sports-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485186-elle?shelf=family-series">family-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485186-elle?shelf=sep">sep</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2485186-elle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer70419543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11952248495901603299">I don't cry when I read books or watch movies (apart from Air Bud, when I was 11) partly because I don't seek out stories that will make me cry, and partly because I have a cold cold heart. But with this book I found more than a few tears rolling down my cheeks. <br/><br/>Maybe this book caught me at a particularly emotional time, but I think not. It is more likely that the complex characters and their unfathomable situations were well written enough to touched me. Deeply. But it wasn't a hopeless type of</span>
  <span id="freeText11952248495901603299" style="display:none">I don't cry when I read books or watch movies (apart from Air Bud, when I was 11) partly because I don't seek out stories that will make me cry, and partly because I have a cold cold heart. But with this book I found more than a few tears rolling down my cheeks. <br /><br />Maybe this book caught me at a particularly emotional time, but I think not. It is more likely that the complex characters and their unfathomable situations were well written enough to touched me. Deeply. But it wasn't a hopeless type of sorrow that was induced within me, the type that can put a storm cloud over your day, but more of a respectful grief for what the characters were dealing with. Best of all even though we know going into this story that there will be a HEA ending, the ending felt completely genuine and realistic.<br /><br />Pluses:<br />- Strongly related to Chicago Stars #3 in its setting but in little else. We are immersed into the Bonner's life and hometown further than with #3 but the characters of #3 take a much more minor role here making this book stand all on it's own and offer a completely different feel then book #3 and yet still be related.<br />- Some great relationship development and personal development. Interesting struggles with realistic resolutions.<br />- Great minor characters and minor romantic plot.<br /><br />Negatives:<br />- Does not have much to do with the Chicago Stars and the football theme. In fact this is more of a branch off book. Some people may be very disappointed about the absence of the football theme but it didn't bother me in the least.<br /><br />I loved this book. It is a heavier piece of fiction than some of the other Chicago Stars books. It is really well written and has excellent characters and plots. My favourite Chicago Stars book use to be #5 based on it's quirkiness but this book has taken the lead. I can see myself rereading this book in full again. Without a question 5 stars. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11952248495901603299" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2777171485" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2777171485" />
    <a title="Lauren" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4731410-lauren"><img alt="Lauren" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387526203p2/4731410.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2777171485?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lauren" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lauren" href="/user/show/4731410-lauren">Lauren</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4731410-lauren?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4731410-lauren?shelf=small-town">small-town</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4731410-lauren?shelf=love-hate-relationship">love-hate-relationship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4731410-lauren?shelf=widows-weeds">widows-weeds</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4731410-lauren?shelf=tortured-hero">tortured-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2777171485" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14699502995512675207"><b>Dream a Little Dream</b><br/>4 Stars<br/><br/>After the loss of his wife and child, Gabe Bonner is only going through the motions of living. That is until Rachel Stone returns to Salvation, North Carolina desperate for a job to support her young son. Despite their rocky start, Rachel and Gabe find themselves inextricably drawn to one another, but can they overcome the traumas of the past to have a future together?<br/><br/><u>Series note:</u> While books 1-3 can be read as standalones, book #4 is a direct continuation of #3 and as</span>
  <span id="freeText14699502995512675207" style="display:none"><b>Dream a Little Dream</b><br />4 Stars<br /><br />After the loss of his wife and child, Gabe Bonner is only going through the motions of living. That is until Rachel Stone returns to Salvation, North Carolina desperate for a job to support her young son. Despite their rocky start, Rachel and Gabe find themselves inextricably drawn to one another, but can they overcome the traumas of the past to have a future together?<br /><br /><u>Series note:</u> While books 1-3 can be read as standalones, book #4 is a direct continuation of #3 and as such the two should be read in order. <br /><br />Rachel is a wonderful heroine. Her strength and resilience in the face of the townsfolk's scorn and shunning are admirable as is her determination to do anything necessary to ensure that her son has everything he needs and deserves. <br /><br />While Gabe has all the making of an excellent tortured hero, there is one aspect of his character that proves very problematic, i.e., his biased attitude and harsh treatment of little Edward. Yes, it is understandable that the sweet little boy reminds Gabe of his dead son, but there are moments when his thoughts and behavior are simply unforgivable. <br /><br />Another problematic issue is the overt Christian themes. While I have nothing against inspirational romance, the focus on God and religion is incongruent with the secular contemporary tone of the series thus far. <br /><br />Despite the abovementioned problems, <b>Dream a Little Dream</b> is a lovely romance with engaging characters who come to life on the page. Make sure to have a box of Kleenex at the ready though because this is one SAD book. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14699502995512675207" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1593215682" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1593215682" />
    <a title="Chitra *CJ*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/46841583-chitra-cj"><img alt="Chitra *CJ*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1479390580p2/46841583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1593215682?book_show_action=true">Mar 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chitra *CJ*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chitra *CJ*" href="/user/show/46841583-chitra-cj">Chitra *CJ*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/46841583-chitra-cj?shelf=scarred-disability">scarred-disability</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/46841583-chitra-cj?shelf=tearjerker">tearjerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/46841583-chitra-cj?shelf=heroines-i-love">heroines-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/46841583-chitra-cj?shelf=safety-first">safety-first</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/46841583-chitra-cj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1593215682" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11656884889051574562">This book..I cant even..WOW.<br/>I mean. PERFECTION.<br/>Two broken souls. One child. The story of finding redemption.<br/>Rachel is the poor, impoverished widow of Dwayne, the leader of a cult group who embezzled the town, Salvation and ran away. She returns to the town destitute, with Edward- her 5 year old son who is a shy, quiet, sad boy.<br/>Gabe, a widower whom we met previously in Cal's book is still shattered and depressed after losing his wife and child and has no drive to live anymore.<br/>When they two meet, </span>
  <span id="freeText11656884889051574562" style="display:none">This book..I cant even..WOW.<br />I mean. PERFECTION.<br />Two broken souls. One child. The story of finding redemption.<br />Rachel is the poor, impoverished widow of Dwayne, the leader of a cult group who embezzled the town, Salvation and ran away. She returns to the town destitute, with Edward- her 5 year old son who is a shy, quiet, sad boy.<br />Gabe, a widower whom we met previously in Cal's book is still shattered and depressed after losing his wife and child and has no drive to live anymore.<br />When they two meet, its not pleasant. Rachel stands tall when life tramples her, and supports herself and her son. She doesn't give up, remains strong, fighting every tear with sarcasm. And she breathes a new life into Gabe.<br />Gabe was a complex character. He loved his first wife Cherry. He loved his son Jamie. Their death hits him very hard. He cannot stop comparing the past with the present. It was great to see him changing throughout the book.<br />The town was really an evil judgmental place- belittling Rachel on every step, blaming her. But nothing broke her spirit.<br />Edward is one of the best and most adorable children ever written. Every "Are we going to die mommy" killed me a little every time- and how his innocence gave a completely new perspective to the characters. Him and his horse stole my heart.<br />The second story is of pastor Ethan and Rachel's housemate and Ethan's assistant Kristy. Kristy has always loved Ethan, who treats her like a sister. With a little boost of confidence from Rachel, she reinvents herself and becomes the woman she could be proud of. And Ethan deals with the calling of god, and then being in love.<br />Half chapter into this book, I knew I was going to cry. And cry I did. But it was angst filled happy tears. Everything about this book simply rocked. And the last half was purely magical.<br />I cant emphasize how much I adore SEP for just writing this. And this remains one of my favorite series ever.<br />Safe read.<br />5/5</span>
  <a data-text-id="11656884889051574562" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aFtvzHRAQquVwywZOPQfCglGYSp604lgnLHM2SiguhXX8orKXf2r6FojgRWHjWoTGnW+WdRZFZdJFFodpCflZg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wal82miJ9BZ1VCKPOOXlYCDZM5BMlUhaTJClwHXrltt+AJncQTQdVbq0j4OHnJB5M+rs4+If1K2ZNTME+WzJqA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer10557116516284107299">SUSAN ELIZABETH PHILLIPS<br/><br/>Susan Elizabeth Phillips is the creator of the sports romance, beginning with her 1989 bestseller, FANCY PANTS. An internationally acclaimed author, her books have been published in over 30 languages. She’s the only four-time recipient of the Romance Writers of America’s prestigious Favorite Book of the Year Award, and a recipient of their Lifetime Achievement Award. <br/><br/>Susan'</span>
  <span id="freeText10557116516284107299" style="display:none">SUSAN ELIZABETH PHILLIPS<br /><br />Susan Elizabeth Phillips is the creator of the sports romance, beginning with her 1989 bestseller, FANCY PANTS. An internationally acclaimed author, her books have been published in over 30 languages. She’s the only four-time recipient of the Romance Writers of America’s prestigious Favorite Book of the Year Award, and a recipient of their Lifetime Achievement Award. <br /><br />Susan's newest book, DANCE AWAY WITH ME, was published in hardcover, ebook and audiobook in June 2020. She is also the highly acclaimed author of both the CHICAGO STARS football series and the Wynette, Texas books. <br /><br />In addition to being a New York Times, Publisher’s Weekly, and USA Today bestseller, she is a hiker, lazy gardener, horrible singer, passable cook, passionate reader, wife, mother of two grown sons, and grandmother. <br /><br />You can visit Susan on Facebook, Twitter, Instagram or on her website.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/SusanElizabethPhillipsNovels">https://www.facebook.com/SusanElizabe...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/sepauthor">https://twitter.com/sepauthor</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/SEPauthor/">https://www.instagram.com/SEPauthor/</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://susanelizabethphillips.com/">http://susanelizabethphillips.com/</a><br /><br /></span>
